Youth Forum

Spring on Jiangwan Road 196

— Guang Mei

The beautiful goddess of spring, with a smile, brought countless gods, happily descended to earth to meet us. Let's not say that everyone is welcoming with joy and excitement. Even the affectionate birds and lovely flowers and trees, aren't they desperately playing with their clever tongues like reeds and strings, vying to spit out their painted and embroidered leaves and pistils. The fluffy fragrant grass, without any hesitation, has woven the vast earth into a pleasing green carpet. The whole world has transformed into a landscape of brocade and embroidery. Ah, whose gift, whose giving, how can we not thank the goddess of spring for bestowing on us - all things with infinite life,

Spring light is routinely scattered on Jiangwan Road. Here there are the intriguing Hongkou Park, 63 Garden and swimming pool, etc. But we should understand that these, these, are all made by our fellow countrymen themselves. They are completely blessed by the foreign masters. Whenever we enjoy these ready-made blessings, we will think of the so-called "park", which is only public to the public. It is pitiful for a group of poor compatriots to taste what the word "public" really means. Although those who can afford to visit the park are not all rich people, they still can't enter without two "Maozi" in their pockets, no matter how much face you have.

Why not, when there are no classes at eight o'clock in the morning, happily go to Jiangwan Road, as smooth as a dance hall, to explore the news of spring. You can see groups of three or five foreign children, carrying schoolbags, as beautiful as flowers, as lively as sparrows, skipping past you "jilugulu", until they turn the corner and are out of sight. Then there are more than sixty members of the running team, bare-legged, no, just a small garment like a swimsuit, full of the vitality of spring, running bravely forward. I, who visited for the first time, was thinking in a daze, I wonder which school this group of athletes is from, oh, or maybe they are from Chi-Zhi. Time does not allow me to think further, they have already sped past me like flying. It turned out to be blue-eyed and yellow-haired gentlemen, ah, their bodies are indeed worthy of being called full of "strength" and "beauty", and it is not an exaggeration to say that the development of their chests is even more impressive than that of our virgins. At that time, I disrespectfully gave birth to a feeling of jealousy towards them. From time to time, you can see the wooden clogs of our close friends, leading a number of small

Continued from page seven

Page 22

Page 23

Page 24

Page 25

students, passing through Jiangwan Road. Presumably, they are going to the countryside for a spring outing. Although they are not wearing uniform uniforms, their country's specialty cloth, red and green, is more attractive than school uniforms, and especially the female teachers walking on both sides, I love the beauty of their buns, their bodies as graceful as jade. This is when I praised those Japanese beauties in Hongkou Park that day, and Hong heard me say that I had a "Daiyu thought".

The sun turned into a red face and was about to shake hands with us and say "see you tomorrow." The moon sister is still a bit virginal after all, hiding alone in the thin curtain. The light breeze blowing on the body is not cold but warm. At this time, this beautiful time, is the golden moment for us to go out for a walk after class and a full meal. At this time, Jiangwan Road is full of fragrant mist. Blue-eyed and yellow-haired gentlemen, wooden clogs "Tuo Tuo" friends, and students from the Law School and Chi-Zhi, are all happily wandering around, or going to the park for a walk. Those in love, of course, honestly and politely walk shoulder to shoulder, smiling and whispering, arrogantly ignoring everything. Those who are not in love are friends of the same sex, and at least three or five are in a group. It seems difficult to see them alone. If you are walking alone in the park, you will never worry about not having one or more foreign-dressed coat racks chasing you before and after, which makes He's heart feel 120 points of displeasure. The day before yesterday, I told Hong angrily about what I encountered in the park. Who knew that not only did I not get her sympathy, but she said, "Who told you to be interesting, like me, I guarantee that no one will come to stare." Haha, God knows, when this day last year, Shu and I were wearing blue cloth overalls, and we didn't use any rouge at all, and we still encountered these guys, which was really annoying.

The sky is gradually getting dark, and we inevitably walk towards the school. At this time, what comes towards us is the large group of silk reeling sisters who are about to get off work. They each carry a food basket, which is the only sign that makes people know them at a glance. I admire them very much, admiring their ability to endure hardship and work hard. The silk reeling sisters of the sacred labor force.

In short, everything is by no means so simple. As long as you take the time to take a walk, what is recorded here is only a group of our spring life. I think when students living in schools in bustling alleys imagine our kind of school life, they may still be so envious that they are drooling. (Guang Mei)

Nanguo Society Art Department Exhibition 197

The Nanguo Society has been immersed in theoretical work, and has had no practical activities in various departments of art for a long time. At this time of spring harmony and bright scenery, in addition to literature, art, music, drama, film and other aspects, there should be some appearances in order. The Art Department plans to hold an exhibition for three days from the 28th to the 30th of this month on the fourth floor of the Ningbo Association, Xizang Road, because the society members Wu Lu and others will cross Europe in April. In addition to the practice and creation of the society members Wang Daoyuan, Liu Gu, Wu Zuoren, Lu Xiaguang, and Liu Ju'an, there are also various support products from society comrades Xu Beihong and Fang Ganmin. The purpose of this exhibition of the society is to liquidate the past gains and losses in art, show the emerging sprouts, and thus promote the close relationship between art and society, and make it a wing of the entire art movement. On the last day (30th), it is also planned to invite local artists to a tea party at the Paris Grand Theater on Avenue Joffre to discuss the path of emerging art.
